<h2 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><b>The Role<\u002Fb><\u002Fh2> \n <div>\n  <p><b>At Shell Energy, we believe that home energy matters. As part of the New Energies team, we are setting up a new business in The Netherlands to support Shell’s ambition to lead in the energy transition towards a low-carbon future through more and cleaner energy solutions. The rapidly evolving retail energy market is a natural place for Shell to expand its business, building on the trusted relationships we have built with our millions of Shell fuel station customers. We aim to grow our customer base by offering an attractive range of products and a real alternative to other companies in the sector through a customer centric and digital approach.<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> Where you fit in<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> We’re looking for a commercially minded and customer focused Customer Experience Analyst. This is a brand-new role within a new corporate start-up that focuses on creating and continuous improving the Customer Journeys for a newly created consumer energy retail business in The Netherlands in 2021. In this role you will report to the Customer Experience Manager and work closely with our customers, the Commercial, Operations and IT\u002FDigital teams.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What’s the role?<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> The Customer Experience Analyst analyzes and interprets applicable data to provide insight and help drive improvement in customer experience. This position focuses on research, data management, report creation and data analysis using a variety of data sources on gaining customer feedback or indicators for journey performance.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> As a corporate start-up, you will be part of a fast-paced organisation. We’ll expect you to be pro-active, collaborative, and hands-on and in return will support and empower you to be successful. Your key accountabilities will include:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> Drive Customer Centricity through customer insights and channel data: Pro-active involvement to ensure that customer centricity is implemented and driven on customer insights together with the CX team in all communications and operational activities. Works closely with the Global New Energies team looking into accelerating customer centricity via customer insights data within Shell.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Customer Experience insights: Help define the Customer Experience we want to give our customers via insights on their needs, jobs to be done and possible delights &amp; dissatisfiers going through our journeys.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Voice of the Customer: Set-up and conduct customer research (surveys, Customer Panel, etc.) to understand customer needs, wants, expectations and preferences and how they perceive our experience.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Data analytics &amp; driver analyses: Analyse customers’ feedback, determine their satisfaction, interpret the results and develop solutions to CX challenges. You also need to define CX measurements and develop ways using tools and platforms for collecting customer experience information cross contact channel. You will come up with proposals on how we can gain better insight into the CX indexes CES, CSAT and how we can influence the drivers behind it.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Customer Journey dashboarding: You create insight into the performance of our customer journey. Support the mapping and maintenance of all Customer Journeys with key insights and performance indicators. Key Customer Journeys evolve around our processes: Onboarding, Live, Renew, Leave and Help Queries.<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What we need from you?<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> You can work and prioritise at pace, in a structure and strategy that’s still being defined. You can operate with a high degree of pragmatism and value momentum and agility over perfection. Furthermore, you have\u002Fare:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> Customer centric mindset: Customer driven and curious to get to know our customers. You are empathic, good listener and you can view our services from customers perspective<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Excellent analytical skills: We are looking for someone with strong analytical skills to study numerous sets of data and translate them to actionable insights. Set-up projects with measurable impact on business, services and customer experience. Therefore, you can use data mining and other analytical techniques to identify and suggest optimization opportunities for the user experience to inform the roadmap of innovation and improvement.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Solid problem-solving skills: As customer experience analyst you will need to be able to solve problems that directly involve an organization’s customers and advise the organization how best to address issues.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Strong communicator: The role requires creative thinking and a real talent for communications. Tasks will involve suggesting ideas based on customer feedback, working with managers and other teams to shape those ideas, then executing. You will also need a blend of good writing, speaking and presentation skills to present customer data in an easy-to-understand manner.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Experience in customer research and tooling: Knowledge and experience of different customer research methodologies (quantitative) including survey set up, Customer panel facilitation, CX indexes (NPS, CSAT, CES) and customer feedback tooling (e.g. GetFeedback). You have:\n    <ul>\n     <li> the ability to plan and conduct quantitative research studies.<\u002Fli>\n     <li> experience in setting up de data involved for our VOC programme and familiarity with survey research techniques and VOC tools.<\u002Fli>\n     <li> strong skills in hypothesis generation, data identification, statistics and testing principles<\u002Fli>\n     <li> the ability to do analytic modeling using methods such as basic statistics, software-assisted segmentation and linear regression.<\u002Fli>\n     <li> the ability to aggregate, standardize, interpret and model data, and to work independently within a data warehouse or decentralized environment.<\u002Fli>\n     <li> are familiar with database queries and programming languages.<\u002Fli>\n     <li> have experience with Web and App analytics platforms to enable omni-channel insights<\u002Fli>\n    <\u002Ful><\u002Fli>\n   <li> Bachelor's Degree Service Design, Business analytics, Economics or Social Science.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> You have substantial experience in similar role or related areas of expertise required for this role.<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> COMPANY DESCRIPTION<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Shell Nederland BV is a platform for international collaboration, with Shell offering direct employment to around ten thousand people in the Netherlands alone, including roughly 2,800 non-Dutch employees from around 80 countries. Diversity is key at Shell Nederland, and our employees reflect the innovation that stems from a diverse workforce. By joining Shell Nederland, you will benefit from an unrivalled industry-leading development programme that will see you tap into a pool of expert knowledge that will help propel your career. Shell Nederland is the holding company of most Shell companies operating in the Netherlands. Shell Nederland also has an advisory and coordinating role in numerous areas.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> An innovative place to work <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>There’s never been a more exciting time to work at Shell.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Join us and you’ll be adding your talent and imagination to a business with the ambition to shape the future – whether by investing in oil, gas and renewable energy to meet demand, exploring new ways to store energy, or developing technology that helps the world to use energy more efficiently, everyone at Shell does their part.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> An inclusive place to work <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>To power progress, we need to attract and develop the brightest minds and make sure every voice is heard. Here are just some of the ways we are nurturing an inclusive environment – one where you can express your ideas, extend your skills, and reach your potential.<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> We’re creating a space where people with disabilities can excel through transparent recruitment process, workplace adjustments and ongoing support in their roles. Feel free to let us know about your circumstances when you apply, and we’ll take it from there.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> We’re closing the gender gap – whether that’s through action on equal pay or by enabling more women to reach senior roles in engineering and technology.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> We’re striving to be a pioneer of an inclusive and diverse workplace, promoting equality for employees regardless of sexual orientation or gender identity.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> We consider ourselves a flexible employer and want to support you finding the right balance. We encourage you to discuss this with us in your application.<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> A rewarding place to work <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>Combine our creative, collaborative environment and global operations with an impressive range of benefits and joining Shell becomes an inspired career choice.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> We’re huge advocates for career development. We’ll encourage you to try new roles and experience new settings. By pushing people to reach their potential, we frequently help them find skills they never knew they had, or make career moves they never thought possible.<\u002Fp>\n  <br> \n <\u002Fdiv>\n <p><\u002Fp> \n <div>\n  <h3 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><p>Disclaimer <\u002Fp><\u002Fh3>\n  <div>\n   <div>\n    Please note: We occasionally amend or withdraw Shell jobs and reserve the right to do so at any time, including prior to the advertised closing date. <h2 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><b>The Role<\u002Fb><\u002Fh2> \n <div>\n  <p>Als Proces Operator bij één van onze fabrieken zorg je ervoor dat het productieproces draaiende wordt gehouden. Je controleert de processen en stelt bij waar nodig. Bij storingen werk je nauw samen met de technische dienst. Je werkt volgens een 2-2-2 volcontinurooster dat geleid word door de Production Team Lead.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Een ploeg bestaat uit één of meer teams die elk verantwoordelijk is voor één of meerdere processen. Een team wordt gevormd door Proces Operators van verschillende functieniveaus.<br> Het is belangrijk dat je beschikt over een goed ontwikkeld verantwoordelijkheidsgevoel voor persoonlijke veiligheid en procesveiligheid met aandacht voor de positie van het bedrijf in de samenleving.<br> Na een inwerkperiode en trainingstraject word je verantwoordelijk voor de normaal voorkomende operationele en relevante niet-operationele werkzaamheden op een aantal onderdelen van een fabriek onder uiteenlopende operationele omstandigheden (normaal bedrijf, starten\u002Fstoppen).<br> Je beoordeelt afwijkingen in de werking van proces en apparatuur en draagt zorg voor het monitoren en bewaken van de condities hiervan. Onderkent in zo vroeg mogelijk stadium mogelijke problemen ten aanzien van veiligheid, milieu, kwaliteit en neemt hierna dienovereenkomstig acties. Je interpreteert analyseresultaten en stelt op grond hiervan zonodig fabriekscondities bij.<br> Tevens zorg je voor een duidelijk verslaggeving tijdens en bij beёindiging van de wacht en voor een goede overdracht van verantwoordelijkheden. Je ziet er op toe dat personeel van uitvoerende diensten conform de op de werkvergunning gestelde condities werken en je neemt zonodig corrigerende maatregelen.<br> Je hebt contact met collega’s, technologen, technische dienst en contractors. Je voert je werkzaamheden zowel zelfstandig als in teamverband uit.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> Wat zoeken wij:<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <div>\n    Wij zoeken mensen met verantwoordelijkheidsgevoel en teamspirit die oplossingsgericht denken, wanneer je nu starter bent of ervaren, wij komen graag met je in contact.\n   <br> \n   <br> Ben jij (binnenkort) in het bezit van een:\n   <br> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Proces Operator C of Allround Operationeel Technicus niveau 4 of in het bezit van een vergelijkbaar diploma VAPRO C theorie en praktijk.<\u002Fli>\n   <\u002Ful>\n   <br> Of:\n  <\u002Fdiv>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li>Ben jij de ervaren Proces Operator B of Allround Operationeel Technicus niveau 3 of in het bezit van een vergelijkbaar diploma VAPRO B theorie en praktijk.<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <br> \n <\u002Fdiv>\n <p><\u002Fp> \n <div>\n  <h3 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><p>Disclaimer <\u002Fp><\u002Fh3>\n  <div>\n   <div>\n    Please note: We occasionally amend or withdraw Shell jobs and reserve the right to do so at any time, including prior to the advertised closing date. <h2 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><b>The Role<\u002Fb><\u002Fh2> \n <div>\n  <p>Shell Asset Management Company B.V. (SAMCo) in The Hague is the dedicated in-house asset manager for the pension funds of the Shell plc group. SAMCo currently manages around USD 80 billion of assets for its clients and has approximately 160 employees. On behalf of its clients, SAMCo invests in fixed income, equities, and alternative investment categories such as private equity and hedge funds, all over the world.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> The 17-people strong Fixed Income department manages the developed market sovereign, emerging market sovereign and corporate credit debt portfolios. Through inhouse research, the team develops a diversified set of fundamental and algorithm-based strategies to meet the clients’ return targets, risk profiles and ESG ambitions. These strategies are implemented using a broad range of instruments, like bonds, loans, interest rate swaps and futures, and credit default swaps.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> We are looking to recruit a <b>Quantitative Analyst <\u002Fb>to join the Fixed Income Department. You will be joining six colleagues focusing on the around EUR 11 billion global portfolio of investment grade and high yield corporate debt, across Europe, the US and emerging market countries.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b><br> What’s the role?<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p> You will be assisting the portfolio management process from day one and thus gain immediate hands-on experience. As a quantitative analyst, you will:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li><p> Maintain existing and develop new quantitative tools to optimize portfolio implementation, like factor premium-based issuer selection, instrument selection and portfolio construction models<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Implement rule-based quantitative strategies<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Contribute to the development of new investment strategies using econometric and machine learning techniques, together with the Artificial Intelligence &amp; Quantitative Research team<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Support the clients’ ESG ambitions by further integrating ESG in the investment process<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Build your network of contacts in the fixed income market, including representatives of banks and brokers, research providers and other asset managers.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><br> In this role you will have a comprehensive on-boarding program, with guidance and support from senior portfolio managers. Due to the breadth and freedom of our mandate we can provide you a broad education of asset management and an opportunity to contribute to the investment process. Naturally, SAMCo will facilitate a VBA or CFA education, as well as support various hard and soft-skill courses.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What we need from you<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p> We are looking for a new colleague with a quantitative background, who has a strong interest in financial markets. We hope to see the following on your resume:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li><p> A Master’s degree in financial mathematics, quantitative economics, the exact sciences or similar education<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Strong programming skills in Python and proficient knowledge of quantitative techniques<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Experience as an analyst, risk manager, data scientist or similar quantitative position is preferred. A finance background is, however, not required if you have a willingness to learn about investing<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> A strong analytical and problem-solving mindset, allowing you to translate theoretical research in implementable strategies, coupled with an ability to work accurately and independently<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Good interpersonal skills and the ability to collaborate well in a team environment with people from a diverse range of backgrounds and cultures<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> A competitive remuneration package based on the prevailing conditions, policies and legislation in the Netherlands will be offered for this position.<\u002Fp>\n  <br> \n <\u002Fdiv>\n <p><\u002Fp> \n <div>\n  <h3 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><p>Disclaimer <\u002Fp><\u002Fh3>\n  <div>\n   <div>\n    Please note: We occasionally amend or withdraw Shell jobs and reserve the right to do so at any time, including prior to the advertised closing date. <h2 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><b>The Role<\u002Fb><\u002Fh2> \n <div>\n  <p><b>Be part of Shell’s ambition in transforming Shell’s Chemicals Park Moerdijk into Europe’s greenest Chemical facility, powering the Energy Transition for and with our customers in North-West Europe. The strategic plans around Energy Transition, Circular feedstocks and Growth are set-up in the ‘North Star Chemical Park Moerdijk. <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b>Where you fit in<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> As one of the world’s leading energy companies, Shell plays a key role in meeting the world’s growing energy demand in economically, environmentally, and socially responsible ways. There has never been a more exciting time to be part of the energy industry. Join us in our ambition to be a net-zero emissions energy business by 2050, and sooner if that is possible.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Shell Chemicals Park Moerdijk is one of the Europe’s leading Chemicals manufacturing locations where using complex processes, base chemicals are produced. Shell Chemicals Park Moerdijk will accelerate the energy transition, be a leader in the sustainable transformation of the chemical industry and grow by making more circular, low-CO2, future-proof products for our customers and society.<\u002Fp>\n  <p> Insulation materials, lightweight plastics, blades for windmills, detergents, mattrasses, batteries, sport shoes – Shell Chemicals Park Moerdijk will become increasingly sustainable when making the chemical building blocks for these type of key products for society<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Thanks to the existing and planned new activities, the number of plants at Shell Chemicals Park Moerdijk may double in the coming decade, while simultaneously we, on balance, aim to no longer emit CO2. In accomplishing this, Shell Chemicals Park Moerdijk joins forces with other companies, customers, employees, organizations, governments, and network operators. Only together as a society we can successfully carry out the transition in the speed that is required. Shell Chemicals Park Moerdijk wants to make a strong effort to help society become more sustainable on a large scale and as quickly as possible.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> The transformation of Shell Chemicals Park Moerdijk offers not only benefits for society but also provides opportunities for employees. There will continue to be new and exciting jobs. The changes are accompanied by innovations and improvements in, for example, the IT field, digitization and development towards new knowledge and activities. This gives employees the opportunity to personally contribute to making society more sustainable.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Together we build the industry of the future!<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What’s the role?<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> The Process Engineer is responsible for the process engineering support to several projects and process engineering support to one of the production units.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Many new projects are started to transform Moerdijk. Implementing the energy transition starts on site. Examples are the plastic to chemicals project, electrification projects, hydrogen projects etc. At the same time the existing operations needs to remain safe, reliable and energy efficient and projects are required to upgrade the existing units and infrastructure. In this role you can experience it all, from design to implementation. The role is an expansion of the team due to the large project workload.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> More specific responsibilities include:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> Work with the production unit of project team on delivering process engineering support and deliverables.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Lead and\u002For assist in development of front-end design packages for small and medium projects. <\u002Fli>\n   <li>Provide strong leadership to the engineering contractors to ensure a safe, operable process design that will meet all the project premises.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Provide process integration when there is a need to integrate a wider range of disciplines when undertaking design activities for projects.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Works as an autonomous Process Engineer, translates the guidelines and standards into practice and solves common technical challenges. Works within company standards and policies under defined directions while receiving occasional guidance on techniques. Makes recommendations and improvements to existing processes. Be knowledgeable in Process Engineering to serve as a Technical Authority to review and approve process technical designs (Technical Assurance) completed by contractors and junior process engineers <\u002Fli>\n   <li>Leading risk screening sessions (DSR\u002FHAZOP) for small projects or large plant changes, being the process safety consciousness.<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> This role is for process engineers who want to bring ideas into practice and like to be involved in many aspects. This an opportunity to experience direct plant support.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What we need from you?<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> We are keen to speak from individuals who have experience in process engineering roles at either operating companies or engineering contractors.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> We also hope you possess the following skills and experience:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> A process engineering education and minimum 5 years working experience in oil and gas or chemicals businesses. (should be able to act on senior process engineering level).<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Affinity with process safety, risk screening and being the process safety consciousness in projects is part of the role<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Capable of leading and integrating multidisciplinary scopes with other discipline engineers and contractors<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Experienced in defining Process Basis of Design<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Curiosity into end-to-end process design, development, and technology maturation<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Attention to process details required to make projects work that meet business objectives, are designed technically safe, meet environmental requirements, are operable and maintainable.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Entrepreneurial, open and curious for industry solutions, making pragmatic use of internal and external standards<\u002Fli>\n   <li> The applicant can execute the position responsibilities with confidence and minimal guidance.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Work experience on a site and Dutch conversation skills is highly beneficial (English will be the main language in the projects, however in the production units Dutch is the main language). For non-Dutch speakers willingness to learn conversational Dutch and language training support will be provided.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> In role you will need to pass a “technical authority” assessment within 6 months.<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> COMPANY DESCRIPTION<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Shell Nederland BV is a platform for international collaboration, with Shell offering direct employment to around ten thousand people in the Netherlands alone, including roughly 2,800 non-Dutch employees from around 80 countries. Diversity is key at Shell Nederland, and our employees reflect the innovation that stems from a diverse workforce. By joining Shell Nederland, you will benefit from an unrivalled industry-leading development programme that will see you tap into a pool of expert knowledge that will help propel your career. Shell Nederland is the holding company of most Shell companies operating in the Netherlands. Shell Nederland also has an advisory and coordinating role in numerous areas.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> An innovative place to work <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>There’s never been a more exciting time to work at Shell.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Join us and you’ll be adding your talent and imagination to a business with the ambition to shape the future – whether by investing in oil, gas and renewable energy to meet demand, exploring new ways to store energy, or developing technology that helps the world to use energy more efficiently, everyone at Shell does their part.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> An inclusive place to work <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>To power progress, we need to attract and develop the brightest minds and make sure every voice is heard. Here are just some of the ways we are nurturing an inclusive environment – one where you can express your ideas, extend your skills, and reach your potential.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> We’re creating a space where people with disabilities can excel through transparent recruitment process, workplace adjustments and ongoing support in their roles. Feel free to let us know about your circumstances when you apply, and we’ll take it from there.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> We’re closing the gender gap – whether that’s through action on equal pay or by enabling more women to reach senior roles in engineering and technology.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> We’re striving to be a pioneer of an inclusive and diverse workplace, promoting equality for employees regardless of sexual orientation or gender identity.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> We consider ourselves a flexible employer and want to support you finding the right balance. We encourage you to discuss this with us in your application.<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> A rewarding place to work <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>Combine our creative, collaborative environment and global operations with an impressive range of benefits and joining Shell becomes an inspired career choice.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> We’re huge advocates for career development. We’ll encourage you to try new roles and experience new settings. By pushing people to reach their potential, we frequently help them find skills they never knew they had, or make career moves they never thought possible.<\u002Fp>\n  <br> \n <\u002Fdiv>\n <p><\u002Fp> \n <div>\n  <h3 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><p>Disclaimer <\u002Fp><\u002Fh3>\n  <div>\n   <div>\n    Please note: We occasionally amend or withdraw Shell jobs and reserve the right to do so at any time, including prior to the advertised closing date. <h2 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><b>The Role<\u002Fb><\u002Fh2> \n <div>\n  <p><b>Where you fit in<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p> You will be part of the new Low Carbon Fuels Team within the Trading &amp; Supply Products organization which is at the heart of Shell’s Downstream business. T&amp;S Products exists as the integrator with the rest of Shell to enable stronger E2E value delivery. Low carbon fuels are a new business within our Trading &amp; Supply Products organization, which is established to enable the delivery of Shell’s low carbon fuels strategy.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What’s the role? <\u002Fb><br> As a Feedstock Originator for South America, you will be accountable to help build a feedstock business with a focus on waste based feedstocks (Used Cooking Oil, Animal Fats and advanced lipids), to supply Shell’s growing portfolio of low carbon fuels plants; initially the role will focus on feedstock supply and trading around the growing HEFA portfolio; long-term the team will also need to supply new and novel feedstocks to a growing range of low carbon fuels processes. Your specific focus will be to short term offtakes, and long-term structured partnerships with waste and agriculture companies to meet Shell’s growing feedstock needs.<\u002Fp>\n  <p> You will report into the Head of HEFA Feedstocks within Shell’s Trading and Supply organization and will need to support a global team of originators, traders, business development managers, supply chain developers and project managers.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Your accountabilities will include:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li><p> Build a material, HEFA feedstock business in South America before 2025.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Scope out and develop long term structural opportunities for feedstock supply in coordination with Shell feedstock traders, with a particular focus on sustainable low carbon feedstocks for supply to HEFA assets.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Close structured offtake deals for feedstocks.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Support the development of optimized in-house and\u002For third-party opportunities, working closely with technology teams to optimize across the asset design \u002F feedstock supply interface.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Take early positions (co-processing, tolling, 3rd party trading) to be able to build a feedstock business before 2025. Work closely with trading colleagues to understand the details of Asian, North American, and European regulations, the impact on supply and demand balances, and develop strategies for optimal supply.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Work with the Biofuel trading desks to optimize the product slate of in-house and\u002For 3rd party assets, to generate maximum end to end margin.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Maintain and deliver a coherent, value driven, LCF strategy for HEFA Feedstock in the region, ensuring alignment across multiple lines of business in Shell.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Maintain a strong Compliance culture and adhere to Shell Business Principles.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What we need from you<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li><p> Previous experience in building a Low Carbon Fuels and HVO\u002FHEFA Feedstocks business will be essential.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Previous experience and track record in structuring long term, complex, commodity deals is essential.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Must have a sound understanding of the Low Carbon Fuel value-chain, and desire to learn the details of LCF products and credit markets. This should include a basic understanding of technical, commercial, and economic considerations.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Previous experience of market analysis, commodity trading, and end-to-end value chain optimization will be essential.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Opportunity Identification: spotting commercial opportunities in the marketplace (rather than just managing existing relationships) and managing these from concept to realization.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Relationship Management: dealing with large customer accounts, governments, and JVs.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Negotiating: leading negotiations and securing complex deals.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Project Management of long-term deals including stakeholder management, both internal and external.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Commercial Skills: including deal-making, contract generation and negotiation; preferably in a trading environment.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Valuation, economics and risk management: candidates should have an understanding and skill in Shell approaches to valuation, economics and risk management.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Deal delivery: candidates should have a track record of deal delivery and project management.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> It is essential that you can show you are a resilient self-starter and can contribute effectively to teamwork, and when required, leading the team without formal authority.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> A proven ability to work in diverse cultural environments is important.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Strong analytical skills, able to interpret data\u002Finformation quickly and translate into actionable business decisions.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Strong commercial acumen and value chain understanding to drive commercial opportunities and improvements.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Proven results delivery capability.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Strong decision-making and problem-solving ability to develop alternative options, solutions and ways of working continuously.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Spanish\u002FPortuguese language preferred, knowledge in English highly advantageous.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> Company Description<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Shell Nederland BV is a platform for international collaboration, with Shell offering direct employment to around ten thousand people in the Netherlands alone, including roughly 2,800 non-Dutch employees from around 80 countries. Diversity is key at Shell Nederland, and our employees reflect the innovation that stems from a diverse workforce. The platform has three key components: Earth for static modelling, Flow for dynamic and surface network modelling and Fusion for integrated reservoir modelling. Thus, PetroSigns contains the applications supporting the range of subsurface development disciplines, including Geosciences, Petrophysics, Reservoir Engineering, Geomechanics and Production Technology. <\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>We are now entering the final stages of PetroSigns development, and the tools are already deployed in several trailblazing assets worldwide, with further deployment to key assets in progress and broader deployment planned. Whereas on a high level the required functionality has been identified, there are still many decisions to be made, both on the level of the constituents Flow and Earth as well as on the integrated functionality and workflows, that will bring large business value.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What’s the role? <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>The purpose of this challenging position is to help further develop the Uncertainty Management capabilities of the PetroSigns platform, harnessing the next-generation static and dynamic modelling applications PetroSigns Earth and PetroSigns Flow to allow multidisciplinary subsurface teams to generate a reliable range of forecasts in support of robust field development decisions.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> The Subsurface Modelling Technology organization develops, deploys and supports Shell’s subsurface technologies in the form of user friendly, commercial grade software. Developing and sustaining these proprietary, differentiating applications requires deep technical skills in technical domains (upstream businesses or R&amp;D) as well as affinity with modern IT.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> The successful candidate will be a Product Owner for one of the software development teams, accountable for:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> Directing technology development and implementation in the area of integrated (static-dynamic) reservoir modelling, focusing on Assisted History Matching and Uncertainty Management<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Further defining and developing proprietary workflows and techniques that support the Shell Multi Scenario Modelling workflow<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Liaising with the Integrated Reservoir Modelling Subject Matter Expert networks to ensure optimal alignment between workflows developed in PetroSigns and business practices<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> This position reports to one of the PetroSigns Product Managers and has no direct reports.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> The selected candidate will be expected to:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> Provide consultancy, and domain leadership for development tasks carried out in the Scrum teams<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Prioritize user requests for enhancements, specifically in uncertainty management<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Interact with end-user and stakeholders to gather requirements for ongoing and future technology developments in PetroSigns<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Help design and drive the implementation of proprietary workflows for history matching and uncertainty quantification in PetroSigns<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Provide 3rd level technical support to the PetroSigns user community, including contributions to technical and user documentation and training materials<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What we need from you<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> We are keen to hear from professionals who have higher education degree in (Petroleum) Engineering, Mathematics or (Earth) Science with subsurface technology research development experience. Beyond that, we’d hope to see as many of the following as possible on your CV:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> Substantial experience in Integrated Reservoir Modelling, history matching and forecasting and ideally some producing asset experience<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Skill and practical experience with Assisted History Matching tools and technologies: experimental design, probability and statistics, ensemble-based methods, optimisation<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Knowledge of business planning and production profiles compilation and full understanding of ullage and facilities impact<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Knowledge of the complex and interdependent set of technologies embodied in technical applications, with skills and experience in several technology application areas, e.g., one or more of Production Geology, Reservoir Engineering, Production Technology or Geomechanics<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Excellent communication and stakeholder management skills, to work effectively with the communities throughout the business<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Affinity with driving the development of large computer applications; experience with, or willingness to learn, working with the agile (Scrum) development process<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Experience with Data Science or Digitalization initiatives would be an advantage<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> We expect to hold interviews for this position in the second week of January.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> Company Description<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Shell Nederland BV is a platform for international collaboration, with Shell offering direct employment to around ten thousand people in the Netherlands alone, including roughly 2,800 non-Dutch employees from around 80 countries. Diversity is key at Shell Nederland, and our employees reflect the innovation that stems from a diverse workforce. By joining Shell Nederland, you will benefit from an unrivalled industry-leading development programme that will see you tap into a pool of expert knowledge that will help propel your career. Shell Nederland is the holding company of most Shell companies operating in the Netherlands. Shell Nederland also has an advisory and coordinating role in numerous areas.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> An innovative place to work <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>There’s never been a more exciting time to work at Shell. <h2 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><b>The Role<\u002Fb><\u002Fh2> \n <div>\n  <p><b>Where you fit in<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Shell aspires to be a global leader in providing cleaner energy solutions to consumers. Trading &amp; Supply is integral to this aspiration and is working with partners in the Downstream to grow its position as a market leader in BioFuels by securing a sizeable and sustainable portfolio of active feedstock positions through our established Global Trading Network, the development of new supply infrastructure while ensuring the business continues to evolve with biofuels legislation, international trade policies and market developments. Shell announced its decision to invest in a brand new and world-scale HEFA facility at the Energy &amp; Chemicals park Rotterdam (Shell Pernis) to process biogenic waste oils and fats into bio-naphtha, renewable diesel and bio-jet. It’s Shell first major step into bio-manufacturing.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><b><br> What’s the role?<br> <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><br> As a Commercial Operator on the Low Carbon Fuel desk you are carrying out the tasks required to meet the contractual obligations of deals agreed by your traders or refinery optimizers. You will liaise with internal departments, customers and other external parties such as third-party operations, brokers and independent surveyors as part of implementing each contract supporting the trading team.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> The Commercial Operator will need to have a solid commercial mindset, you will have the freedom and opportunity to significantly contribute to the profitability of the product trading team. Next to this you need to demonstrate solid team working skills and have self-starter qualities. Be able to work accurately and focused under pressure and will exhibit strong communication skills. The willingness to assume responsibility for and ownership and accountability of his\u002Fher tasks is essential.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Modes of transport that you will be operating are very diverse. Contracts can be executed via waterways on barge and vessels. But you will also be operating contracts via truck, train, container and flexibags.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What we need from you?<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> We’re keen to hear from professionals who have a bachelor’s degree or equivalent work experience. Beyond that, we’d hope to see as many of the following as possible on your CV:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> Effective interpersonal skills, problem solving mentality and quick decision making;<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Substantial experience with storage, handling and transport on a wide array of BioFuels;<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Complete understanding of all factors that influence profit and loss and exposure. And ability to translate traders strategy to operational plan. Part of this role might entail blending activities on different terminals.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> End-to-end understanding on how value is created in the biofuels business such as supply chain network design and cost optimization;<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Knowledge of international import\u002Fexport trade practices;<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Excellent communication, presentation, and stakeholder management skills.<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> COMPANY DESCRIPTION<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Shell Nederland BV is a platform for international collaboration, with Shell offering direct employment to around ten thousand people in the Netherlands alone, including roughly 2,800 non-Dutch employees from around 80 countries. Diversity is key at Shell Nederland, and our employees reflect the innovation that stems from a diverse workforce. By joining Shell Nederland, you will benefit from an unrivalled industry-leading development programme that will see you tap into a pool of expert knowledge that will help propel your career. Shell Nederland is the holding company of most Shell companies operating in the Netherlands. Shell Nederland also has an advisory and coordinating role in numerous areas.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> An innovative place to work<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> There’s never been a more exciting time to work at Shell. Everyone here is helping solve one of the biggest challenges facing the world today: bringing the benefits of energy to everyone on the planet, whilst managing the risks of climate change.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Join us and you’ll add your talent and imagination to a business with the power to shape the future – whether by investing in renewables, exploring new ways to store energy or developing technology that helps the world to use energy more efficiently.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> An inclusive place to work<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> To power progress together, we need to attract and develop the brightest minds and make sure every voice is heard. Here are just some of the ways we’re nurturing an inclusive environment – one where you can express your ideas, extend your skills and reach your potential.<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> We’re creating a space where people with disabilities can excel through transparent recruitment process, workplace adjustments and ongoing support in their roles. Feel free to let us know about your circumstances when you apply and we’ll take it from there.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> We’re closing the gender gap – whether that’s through action on equal pay or by enabling more women to reach senior roles in engineering and technology.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> We’re striving to be a pioneer of an inclusive and diverse workplace, promoting equality for employees regardless of sexual orientation or gender identity.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> We consider ourselves a flexible employer and want to support you finding the right balance. We encourage you to discuss this with us in your application.<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> A rewarding place to work<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Combine our creative, collaborative environment and global operations with an impressive range of benefits and joining Shell becomes an inspired career choice.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> We’re huge advocates for career development. We’ll encourage you to try new roles and experience new settings. By pushing people to reach their potential, we frequently help them find skills they never knew they had, or make career moves they never thought possible.<\u002Fp>\n  <br> \n <\u002Fdiv>\n <p><\u002Fp> \n <div>\n  <h3 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><p>Disclaimer <\u002Fp><\u002Fh3>\n  <div>\n   <div>\n    Please note: We occasionally amend or withdraw Shell jobs and reserve the right to do so at any time, including prior to the advertised closing date. support for the Shell Energy and Chemicals Park Rotterdam. Based in Pernis, you will work in a team of other civil engineers in a multidisciplinary environment to manage the integrity of the civil assets. The civil scope covers: Geotechnical &amp; Structural (concrete\u002Fsteel) structures, Civil drainage systems, buildings, nautical facilities, tank pits, (rail) roads, Insulation &amp; Coating (Fabric) design, Fire &amp; Explosion protection design, Refractory and Liquid containing structures.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> More specific responsibilities include:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> Actively contribute to the Front End Loading in the initiate and assess phase of projects.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Assure the civil aspects in projects following the DECAF process.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Assure compliance with civil external and internal standards.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Assure the civil aspects in plant changes within projects.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Perform engineering checks and give engineering support to your colleagues in the department.<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What we need from you?<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> We’re keen to hear from individuals with relevant experience in the field of civil maintenance or projects (preferably in Oil &amp; Gas). Shell Nederland is the holding company of most Shell companies operating in the Netherlands. Shell Nederland also has an advisory and coordinating role in numerous areas.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> An innovative place to work <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>There’s never been a more exciting time to work at Shell.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Join us and you’ll be adding your talent and imagination to a business with the ambition to shape the future – whether by investing in oil, gas and renewable energy to meet demand, exploring new ways to store energy, or developing technology that helps the world to use energy more efficiently, everyone at Shell does their part.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> An inclusive place to work <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>To power progress, we need to attract and develop the brightest minds and make sure every voice is heard. The Customer Journey is at the heart of what we do, to drive the appropriate processes and customer experience, aligning to the risk controls of the business. providers and rail transport companies in line with Shell Chemicals and Products business requirements.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> In this role you are working on the existing chemical product portfolio, as well on the circular plastics projects, sustainability service offering and bio based chemical solutions. In this changing world the contract manager will be the logistics expert and acquire the right services for Shell Chemicals business.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What’s the role?<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p> You sit within the Logistics Team with Chemicals and Products North West Europe, responsible for the full logistical footprint of Shell Chemicals. This is a key role to ensure the logistics needs for our Chemicals business are met with by partnering with LSPs to curate a safe, reliable, robust, and competitive supply chain. Worthy to highlight that the European logistics market (road\u002Frail transportation, storage, freight forwarding, drumming) are of a multi-billion turn-over. These are very mature markets with LSP’s servicing a wide variety of businesses, including the Chemicals liquid business. This requires a prudent and mature logistics Contract Manager who can ensure that Chemicals specific logistics needs are correctly executed. Further you as Contract Manager need to develop and maintain effective relationship networks in that market to ensure latest developments and its impact are well understood by Shell.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> You procure logistics services and manage the performance of contracted Logistics Service Providers in cooperation with relevant stakeholders. You are responsible to ensure that the Shell Chemicals logistics requirements are translated into the appropriate logistics contracts for services provided by LSP’s and you will lead contract negotiations with LSP’s.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> In addition, you will manage term contracts by developing contract strategy papers and effective Best Alternative to a Negotiated Agreement. This role also needs to ensure an effective contract management process to deliver the maximum value of the contract in place and provide assurance for compliance against all contractual agreed terms, HSSE standards and minimum requirements with the LSPs. This includes stretching the HSSE performance to what good looks like and constantly evolve into a generative HSSE standards and performance.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> As appointed Contract Holder, it is key to understand the responsibilities under the Chemicals management system and act accordingly plus deliver the LSP engagement plan and work with contractors to meet the HSSE and Operational performance KPI's. We are also looking for someone who will bring contractor management to the next level in terms of creating value for the business and reduce transactional costs in the relationship with the contractors. Furthermore, in the spirit of customer centricity, you need to apply a mindset of continuous improvement to structurally solve operational problems and initiate improvements, including accountable to resolve complaints and claims in relation to the Logistics Service Providers and in-time payment to LSP’s.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What we need from you?<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> Bachelor’s or Master’s degree preferably in a logistics or commercial discipline<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Experience in a logistics procurement role or a commercial role and relevant background in rail transport and\u002For storage operations<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Commercial acumen and ability to translate technical and logistics requirements into operational and contractual agreements is a key requirement<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Healthy commercial and good relationship with logistics service providers (LSP) and adopt a continuous improvement focus<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Learner mindset<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Good communication skills, fluency in English<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Good analytical skills<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Problem solving abilities to improve our business daily<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> Compaby Description<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Shell Nederland BV is a platform for international collaboration, with Shell offering direct employment to around ten thousand people in the Netherlands alone, including roughly 2,800 non-Dutch employees from around 80 countries. SE-EE was created in 2009 through the combination of Shell’s marketing and trading companies in Europe. SE-EE is part of Shell Energy which is the commercial heart of the Integrated Gas Business and aligns all Energy Trading activity throughout the world.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> As part of the SE-EE and NEs growth strategy, Power and Gas wholesale and customer activities are scaling significantly in existing and expanding into new market areas and deal types. This involves a significant amount of work on selecting, integrating, and maintaining new systems and processes.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Shell Energy Europe Ltd. (SE-EE) acts as the Balancing Responsible Party (BRP) for renewable assets operated across Europe. This involves consolidating for varying local markets long and short positions to net off imbalance positions, minimise value leakage, and maximise value creation opportunity against the system price. Data is critically important in this process to inform optimisation of forecasts and to predict system buyout price. Different markets have different regulatory regimes related to the balancing market and a deep understanding of each market is critical to ensure continued license to operate for SE-EE, and maximising value for the end-to-end business.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What’s the role? <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>The primary accountabilities of the Renewable Data Analyst (Power) are:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li><p> Work in a team of multiple Data Analysts to validate and correct data to support business critical processes.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Keep track of Shell Energy Europe Ltd.’s Portfolio in SE-EE’s data management solution(s).<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Collect, process, and analyse operational data (including measurement, allocation, imbalance, and reconciliation data) in order to report to internal and external stakeholders.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Troubleshoot issues with internal and external counterparties, including Grid Operators.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Anomalies in generation and consumption patterns investigated and understood.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Actively manage relationships with internal and external stakeholders (including relevant market organizations)<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Facilitate necessary management approvals.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Work to standardise, and automate as many of these processes as possible in conjunction with IT.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Understand the deal funnel to assess and manage the workload associated with integrating new opportunities into relevant systems.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Deep understanding of balancing regimes in country, well connected with regulatory bodies, able to understand upcoming regulatory changes and able to coordinate teams to implement system and process changes ahead of new introduction of new and\u002For changed rules.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What we need from you<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> The successful candidate would be required to:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li><p> Be inspired by and committed to the success of Shell in the Energy Transition.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Be comfortable with big, complex data sets, analysis, and application of that data to drive business value.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Can process large data sets through building own queries to support resolve complex issues and support decision making.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Show a keen interest in IT\u002Fdigitalization and other technology advancements and how these can be applied to drive competitive advantage in Shell.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Understand the end-to-end Life of a Deal process in SE-EE.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Excellent customer service\u002Fattention\u002Fmanner.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Ability to scope and manage changes to IT projects and drive process improvements.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Have experience in regulatory reporting frameworks for Power in Europe, demonstrating an interest in balancing regimes.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Develop business relationships with customers and IT vendors.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Operate effectively as part of a team as well as autonomously.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Adapt quickly to a dynamic environment and demonstrate resilience under pressure.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> The successful candidate should also possess the following skills:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li><p> Very strong interpersonal and communication skills (fluent in spoken and written English, Dutch is also preferred).<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Excellent stakeholder engagement.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Highly analytical, data driven with strong attention to detail.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> Process Improvement mindset.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n   <li><p> A basic knowledge of Trading and Supply European Power Operations, Trade Finance and Controls, European Regulatory Reporting and Compliance.<\u002Fp><\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> Company for Shell Nederland Chemie B.V. (SNC). Based in Moerdijk,you will work in a multidisciplinary environment to manage the civil assets for our 4 world scale production units (MLO, MVEO, MSPO1 and 2) including the Filling and Dispatch and General Facilities. The civil scope covers concrete and steel structures, civil drainage, and cooling water systems, NRB provisions, buildings, jetties and marine structures, tank pits, rail and roads, insulation &amp; coating, refractory, fire &amp; explosion protection and soil &amp; groundwater management.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> More specific responsibilities include:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> Responsible for the integrity of the wide range of civil assets.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Perform inspections and detail scope to remediate the findings where required.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Develop and implement strategies for extraordinary maintenance via Asset Integrity Masterplanning (AIMP) or via the Project Route.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Support maintenance and Turn Around (TA) activities in close collaboration with the Production Unit teams.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Resolve engineering queries with the Production Unit teams, but you will also bring the civil medium- and long-term programs in the plan for the Production Unit.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Regular presence on site to verify HSSE compliant execution and general quality assurance verification is expected.<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What we need from you?<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> We are keen to speak to individuals with relevant experience in the field of civil engineering (preferably in Oil &amp; Gas). Diversity is key at Shell Nederland, and our employees reflect the innovation that stems from a diverse workforce. By joining Shell Nederland, you will benefit from an unrivalled industry-leading development programme that will see you tap into a pool of expert knowledge that will help propel your career. Shell Nederland is the holding company of most Shell companies operating in the Netherlands. Shell Nederland also has an advisory and coordinating role in numerous areas.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> An innovative place to work <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>There’s never been a more exciting time to work at Shell.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Join us and you’ll be adding your talent and imagination to a business with the ambition to shape the future – whether by investing in oil, gas and renewable energy to meet demand, exploring new ways to store energy, or developing technology that helps the world to use energy more efficiently, everyone at Shell does their part.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> An inclusive place to work <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>To power progress, we need to attract and develop the brightest minds and make sure every voice is heard. <h2 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><b>The Role<\u002Fb><\u002Fh2> \n <p><\u002Fp>\n <div>\n  <p><b>What’s the role? <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>The Bio-feedstock Researcher is a scientist role in the Bio-Technology team, responsible for leading and supporting multiple research projects. Activities are focused on delivering low carbon options and Biofuels into the market; as well as developing broader topical, project and market expertise related to multiple forms of energy. The team are part of Shell Projects and Technology Chemicals, Downstream Process and Bio-Technology organization. It seeks to solve key scientific challenges to support technologies; that unlock new business opportunities for Shell in Low Carbon Fuels, New Energies and Chemicals.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> The program is focused on delivering low carbon biofuels, chemicals and natural carbon sinks into the market. The role is to define the research and deliver to the Shell businesses novel bioprocesses, which cost effectively convert renewable feedstocks to biofuels\u002Fchemicals via fermentation or anaerobic digestive routes. In addition, the role supports activities which sequester CO2 into natural ecosystems.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Key accountabilities: <\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>The Bio-feedstock Researcher will lead research, due diligence, market intelligence and business steer on renewable molecules; that better harness energy and atmospheric carbon, through novel hosts, feedstocks, pathways and processes, including fermentation, solid state systems\u002Fanaerobic digestion.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> The challenges in this role range from key and deep scientific questions to option identification and external due diligence for the businesses, in the areas of biological hosts, agronomy, fermentation optimization\u002Fscale up, solid and liquid phase fermentation to novel feedstocks\u002Fconversion systems.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Dimensions:<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Potential candidates will be engaged in and lead a range of activities and projects in areas such as:<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> Anaerobic fermentation, agronomy, feedstock availability, bio process design and optimization and host organism research both internally and externally<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Design and implementation of experimental programs aimed at producing commercially viable biofuel and\u002For chemicals from micro-organisms and biological feedstocks, considering wide range of contributory factors, identifying opportunities and engaging with the development of commercial plans<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> The candidate leads activities in support of the Long-Range Research platform, ensuring alignment of research activities to long term business strategy. The successful candidate will be expected to work with Shell businesses, engineers (as well as) with external partners.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What we need from you<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Candidates are expected to have excellent intellectual and analytical ability. The enthusiasm to progress their insights, strong teamwork and leadership skill; as well as the ability to broaden outside of their area of expertise.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Key Skills and Requirements:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> PhD in one of the following areas or related field:\n    <ul>\n     <li> Agronomy<\u002Fli>\n     <li> Agricultural Engineering<\u002Fli>\n     <li> Biological Engineering<\u002Fli>\n     <li> Ecology<\u002Fli>\n     <li> Forestry<\u002Fli>\n     <li> Horticulture<\u002Fli>\n     <li> Plant Breeding<\u002Fli>\n    <\u002Ful><\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> Experience in one or more of the following areas would be a distinct advantage: Practical knowledge of biological process design and scale up, fermentation and agronomy, hands-on expert working knowledge of a biological discipline<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Knowledge of sugars\u002Flipids to biofuels conversion technologies, enzyme hydrolysis and solid and\u002For liquid fermentation (batch or continuous flow at pilot scale)<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Demonstrated willingness to learn and apply cross-discipline approaches to solving problems and be happy working in a tight-knit team<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Excellent written and verbal communication skills<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Ability to contribute cooperatively to a highly collaborative and team-oriented environment<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> Company Description<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Shell Nederland BV is a platform for international collaboration, with Shell offering direct employment to around ten thousand people in the Netherlands alone, including roughly 2,800 non-Dutch employees from around 80 countries. Shell<\u002Fb><\u002Fp> \n  <p>Lekker aan de slag bij Shell, op momenten dat het jou uitkomt, dat klinkt goed, toch? Je werkt in een gezellig team op een tankstation bij jou in de buurt. Je vindt het mooi om je gasten blij te maken. Met een lekkere kop koffie, thee, frisdrank, een broodje of een warme snack. Door snel en netjes de brandstof af te rekenen. Zo gaan ze blij weer op pad, en komen ze terug!<\u002Fp> \n  <p>Iedereen die bij delibyShell binnenkomt, is een belangrijke gast. Of ze alleen een snel kopje koffie halen of iets lekkers voor het hele gezin of het complete zangkoor, hun ervaring bepaalt of ze met een glimlach op hun gezicht verder reizen. En dat is precies waar jij en collega horecamedewerkers in beeld komen.<\u002Fp> \n  <p>Even opladen of bijtanken, dat is wat duizenden gasten ieder uur doen bij Shell. En wat wij ze bieden, is een topervaring. Onze tankstations en delibyShells zijn het beste wat de markt te bieden heeft. Bij ons ligt de lat hoog, en dat merk je zodra je binnenkomt.<\u002Fp> \n  <p>Als jij een leuke bijbaan zoekt, is delibyShell een hele goede keus.<br> Krijg je al trek om lekker bij ons aan de slag te gaan?<\u002Fp> \n  <p><b>Wie ben je<\u002Fb><\u002Fp> \n  <ul>\n   <li>Een vriendelijk gezicht, als jij 'goedemorgen', 'goedemiddag' of goedenavond' zegt, voelt jouw gast zich welkom. Je bent gastheer\u002Fgastvrouw én verkoper.<\u002Fli> \n   <li>Handig en snel zorg je ervoor dat de klant afrekent. Vriendelijk breng je de speciale voordeelaanbiedingen onder de aandacht.<\u002Fli> \n   <li>Contant, betaalpassen, tankpassen en creditcards, jij zorgt ervoor dat de klant gemakkelijk en snel afrekent.<\u002Fli> \n   <li>Alsof het je eigen tankstation is. Met aandacht voor iedereen, netjes, vrolijk. Blij met iedere euro die de klant bij jou afrekent. Altijd een vriendelijk woord. Als het rustig is, vul je de schappen bij.<\u002Fli> \n   <li>Je voelt aan wat je gast wilt, doet passende suggesties en bent aardig voor je gasten.<\u002Fli> \n   <li>Je bent een fijne collega die graag in een team werkt. Want je weet, samen kom je verder.<\u002Fli> \n  <\u002Ful> \n  <p><b>Wat doe je<\u002Fb><\u002Fp> \n  <ul>\n   <li>Druk druk, gezellig druk. Houd er maar rekening mee dat het druk is, soms heel druk, in de ochtend- en de avondspits. En ook dan ben jij vriendelijk, vrolijk, precies en snel.<\u002Fli> \n   <li>Je voelt aan dat sommige gasten zo snel mogelijk verder willen, en dat andere gasten iets meer tijd nemen. <h2 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><b>The Role<\u002Fb><\u002Fh2> \n <div>\n  <p><b>Be part of Shell’s ambition in transforming Shell’s Chemicals Park Moerdijk into Europe’s greenest Chemical facility, powering the Energy Transition for and with our customers in North-West Europe. The strategic plans around Energy Transition, Circular feedstocks and Growth are set-up in the ‘North Star Chemical Park Moerdijk. <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b>Where you fit in<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> As one of the world’s leading energy companies, Shell plays a key role in meeting the world’s growing energy demand in economically, environmentally, and socially responsible ways. There has never been a more exciting time to be part of the energy industry. Join us in our ambition to be a net-zero emissions energy business by 2050, and sooner if that is possible.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Shell Chemicals Park Moerdijk is one of the Europe’s leading Chemicals manufacturing locations where using complex processes, base chemicals are produced. Shell Chemicals Park Moerdijk will accelerate the energy transition, be a leader in the sustainable transformation of the chemical industry and grow by making more circular, low-CO2, future-proof products for our customers and society.<\u002Fp>\n  <p> Insulation materials, lightweight plastics, blades for windmills, detergents, mattrasses, batteries, sport shoes – Shell Chemicals Park Moerdijk will become increasingly sustainable when making the chemical building blocks for these type of key products for society<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Thanks to the existing and planned new activities, the number of plants at Shell Chemicals Park Moerdijk may double in the coming decade, while simultaneously we, on balance, aim to no longer emit CO2. In accomplishing this, Shell Chemicals Park Moerdijk joins forces with other companies, customers, employees, organizations, governments, and network operators. Only together as a society we can successfully carry out the transition in the speed that is required. Shell Chemicals Park Moerdijk wants to make a strong effort to help society become more sustainable on a large scale and as quickly as possible.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> The transformation of Shell Chemicals Park Moerdijk offers not only benefits for society but also provides opportunities for employees. There will continue to be new and exciting jobs. The changes are accompanied by innovations and improvements in, for example, the IT field, digitization and development towards new knowledge and activities. This gives employees the opportunity to personally contribute to making society more sustainable.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Together we build the industry of the future!<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What’s the role?<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> The Technical Safety Engineer will support the large energy transition and circular economy projects on site Moerdijk. The technical safety engineer will be part of the Process Safety and Process Engineering team, which provides process safety and process engineering support to the production units in Moerdijk. The role is an expansion of the team due to the large project workload.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> This role has the following accountabilities:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> Lead, participate, plan, organize and scribe HSE risk assessment workshops and studies, including HAZIDs, HAZOPs, LOPA, PSSR, Physical Effects Modelling and ALARP assessments<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Deliver the overall ALARP demonstration report for projects<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Identify and judge the risk of facilities\u002Fdesign and advise practical solutions to reduce such risks.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Assist in resolving any discrepancies in the safety aspects of the design standard by practicable and cost-effective solutions and recommendations<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Provide support for the management and health of process safety barriers, HSSE critical equipment as well as HSSE critical activities<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Support \"Fit-for-purpose\" implementation of Global HSSE Standards and develop and maintain applicable procedures and guidelines<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Provides expert advice and input to projects and operations on the Hazard and Effects Management Process (HEMP) in order to meet ALARP<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Participate in incident investigations, audits and Go and Sees<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> What we need from you?<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> We are keen to speak to individuals with process engineering, technical safety engineering or similar background. You must have proven experience in a process engineering, technical safety or process safety related function.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> We also hope you possess the following skills and experience:<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> A technical education in preferably process engineering or similar<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Ability to think and communicate in scenarios and barriers<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Working knowledge of technical risk assessment tools such as HAZID, HAZOP, LOPA, physical effects modelling, Fire safety.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Working knowledge in work processes like management of change, Instrument protective functions, Emergency response, ensure safe production.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Experience with applying relevant industry codes related to process safety<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Strong verbal communication and technical writing skills<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Ability to work within teams<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Ability to facilitate process safety assessments like HAZOP, LOPA, PSSR<\u002Fli>\n   <li> Work experience on a site and Dutch conversation skills is highly beneficial (English will be the main language in the projects). For non-Dutch speakers willingness to learn conversational Dutch and language training support will be provided.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> In role you will need to pass a “technical authority” assessment within 12 months.<\u002Fli>\n  <\u002Ful>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> COMPANY DESCRIPTION<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Shell Nederland BV is a platform for international collaboration, with Shell offering direct employment to around ten thousand people in the Netherlands alone, including roughly 2,800 non-Dutch employees from around 80 countries. Diversity is key at Shell Nederland, and our employees reflect the innovation that stems from a diverse workforce. By joining Shell Nederland, you will benefit from an unrivalled industry-leading development programme that will see you tap into a pool of expert knowledge that will help propel your career. Shell Nederland is the holding company of most Shell companies operating in the Netherlands. Shell Nederland also has an advisory and coordinating role in numerous areas.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> An innovative place to work <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>There’s never been a more exciting time to work at Shell.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p> Join us and you’ll be adding your talent and imagination to a business with the ambition to shape the future – whether by investing in oil, gas and renewable energy to meet demand, exploring new ways to store energy, or developing technology that helps the world to use energy more efficiently, everyone at Shell does their part.<\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p><b> An inclusive place to work <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n  <p><\u002Fp>\n  <p>To power progress, we need to attract and develop the brightest minds and make sure every voice is heard. Here are just some of the ways we are nurturing an inclusive environment – one where you can express your ideas, extend your skills, and reach your potential.<\u002Fp>\n  <ul>\n   <li> We’re creating a space where people with disabilities can excel through transparent recruitment process, workplace adjustments and ongoing support in their roles. Feel free to let us know about your circumstances when you apply, and we’ll take it from there.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> We’re closing the gender gap – whether that’s through action on equal pay or by enabling more women to reach senior roles in engineering and technology.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> We’re striving to be a pioneer of an inclusive and diverse workplace, promoting equality for employees regardless of sexual orientation or gender identity.<\u002Fli>\n   <li> We consider ourselves a flexible employer and want to support you finding the right balance.
